  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.6)
    The story effectively uses symbolism (pressed penny, mirror reflection) to explore themes of self-deception and reconciliation. The central conflict between perceived reality and truth creates meaningful tension. However, the resolution feels somewhat predictable, and the dialogue in the climactic scene lacks the subtlety present in the earlier descriptive passages. The story shows rather than tells, but could delve deeper into emotional nuance.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=3.9)
    The story attempts thematic depth (communication, unity) and uses some symbolism (lamp). However, the craft is severely undermined by the inconsistent and illogical use of the phrase 'earnest mockery'. This phrase, critical to the prompt's constraints, is misused, repeated awkwardly, and ultimately makes the concluding sentence nonsensical, destroying narrative credibility. Dialogue is minimal and functional. Showing vs. telling is inconsistent; emotions are often stated directly.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.5)
